7/21/20, 7:06 PM - piyush bhujbal: -Dear Learners,
 
A very Warm Greetings from *All India Council for Technical Education & AISSMS College of Engineering, Pune and Institution of Engineers (India), Kolkata..!!!*.

           The world today is facing an unprecedented crisis in the form of COVID-19, but it is necessary not to forget that a bigger crisis in terms of climate change is looming over the world. The primary cause for climate change has been attributed to the Energy Paradox that the world faces today, wherein more energy is required to achieve and maintain high economic growth rates, while rampant use of energy is causing climate change.

 There is a FREE Online Multidisciplinary course under the aegis of Energy Swaraj Foundation to “Design a Solar System for Homes”.

          Any student above the age of 14 years can take up this course. The course does not require much technical background and can be completed in less than 3 hours. AICTE looks forward to your participation in making the students across the globe Energy Literate.

 Please note that there are no manpower or cost requirements for the course.

        This course gives a unique opportunity to become Energy Literate irrespective of your educational background and experience.

Please see the below details for sharing with the students of the organization:

College Login Page:

Link for Registration:

https://energyswaraj.org/take-quiz.php?organization_id=organization_836

 

In order to successfully complete the course, the students need to carefully watch 15 videos that are available both in English and Hindi. After watching the videos, the students are expected to take a quiz. Students, who will successfully complete the course, will get the certificates. This certificate may be useful for students for their future prospects.
 

 

Note: Kindly ensure maximum Students, Faculties and Non-Teaching staff will register for the course and submit the list of students registered

 



Contact Person: Prof. Nitin Mawale, Coordinator for this Activity 

(Mobile No: 9764248929  Email Id: npmawale@aissmscoe.com)

 



 Instructions to be followed:

Any student above the age of 14 years can take up this course.
 Participants Institute/College/HighSchool Name is Not Required. 
 It is a self-paced course.
  There are 15 videos in the course. Students need to watch each and every video to successfully complete the course.
 Students must clear the quiz to get the certificate.
 There are in total 32 questions of 40 marks. To clear the quiz you need to score at least 25 marks to be eligible for the certificate.
 Only 2 Quiz attempts per participant will be allowed.


Forward the mail to all Students, Faculties and Non-teaching Staff. All can take this 3 Hours Course.
  
Please do the needful on urgent basis.

Thanking you,

Regards,

Coordinator:
Prof. Nitin Mawale

Dr D G Bhalke

Dr. D S Bormane

Hey Geek,

Greetings from the Rajarambapu Institute of Technology, Rajaramnagar, RIT - IEEE Chapter, and RIT-CS-MAC Club.
Hope you are doing well.

We believe that learning is a continuous process and must continue even in the toughest times such as this pandemic.
With this in mind, we invite you for a Virtual Skill Enhancement Program called Week For Geeks.
This program gives you an opportunity to develop your skills in any of the following tracks,

1. Machine Learning.
2. Android Application Development
3. Web Development.
4. Cloud Computing.

And the best part- it's Free of Cost and gets you Internship opportunities!!!

The program takes place in 3 Stages,

1. Learning with Implementation
2. Developing a Mini Project
3. Competing with the Community

We believe that we learn better when we implement it, and thus the program's design is such that participants implement what they learn.

Why This Program :
1. Internship Opportunities in top Software Firms.
2. Guidance and Support from the mentors.
3. Build a community of the geekiest minds.
4. Steps towards a new career path.

Commences On : 15th Sept. 2020
Duration : 7+7 Days

11/24/20, 10:27 AM - ꜱʜʀᴇʏᴀꜱʜ ᴍᴜʟᴀʏ: from array import *
def Marks_database():
    total_students=int(input('Enter the total no. of students in the class:'))
    FDS()
    num = int(input('No. of students present in exam:'))
    for i in range (num):
         FDS.append (int(input('Enter the Marks of student:')))
    print('Avg. no. of students:',sum(FDS)/num)
    print('Highest marks Scored in Exam:',max(FDS))
    print('Lowest marks Scored in Exam:',min(FDS))
    absent = total_students-num
    print('Absent students for exam:',absent)
    print('The most frequent marks scored are:',max(set(FDS),key=FDS.count))
Marks_database()

The Design Innovation Centre (DIC) & Institution's Innovation Council (IIC) 3.0 Savitribai Phule Pune University (SPPU) are in collaboration with BVB Muktangan Exploratory, Pune organizing an Innovative Toys/Games Design Competition "Khel Khel Mein" based on Indian Values, Culture & Heritage.

In this event, students can showcase their toys/games/project designs. 

Who Can Participate?

Student/s having innovative toys/games/ project ideas or design can participate in this mega event.  

The event is scheduled on 28th February 2021 in online mode.

For Registration kindly visit at  https://events.unipune.ac.in/sites/Khel_Kehl_Mein/

Last date of registration: 15th February 2021.

Note: This is a free event (No registration fee)

Please find the attached flyer for your reference and circulate with your students and faculty so it can reach to large no of students.

Best Regards, 
Design Innovation Centre,

name=input("welcome pleaase Enter name")

num=0
print("Mr.",name,"Here is some suggetions    1)Science and tech.    2)Chatrapati Shivaji Maharaj")
choice=int(input("enter choice"))
if choice==1:
    str1="What Is Information Science?   You might have questions about what we mean when we say “information science.” Information science includes any professional who works with, researches about, or learns about the management of information in any form. Whether you are interested in storing, retrieving, describing, organizing, representing, or providing information to others, ASIS&T is for you!Here are a few definitions of information science from leaders in our field:“Information science is that discipline that investigates the properties and behavior of information, the forces governing the flow of information, and the means of processing information for optimum accessibility and usability. It is concerned with the body of knowledge relating to the origination, collection, organization, storage, retrieval, interpretation, transmission, and utilization of information.”— Borko, H. (1968). Information science: What is it? American Documentation, 19, 3.“… information science brings together and uses the theories, principles, techniques and technologies of a variety of disciplines toward the solution of information problems.  Among the disciplines brought together in this amalgam called information science are computer sciences, cognitive science, psychology, mathematics, logic, information theory, electronics, communications, linguistics, economics, classification science, systems science, library science and management science.  They are brought to bear in solving the problems with information — its generation, organization, representation, processing, distribution, communication and use.”— Williams, M. E. (1987/1988). Defining information science and the role of ASIS. Bulletin of the American Society for Information Science, 14(2), 17-“Information science is the science and practice dealing with the effective collection, storage, retrieval, and use of information. It is concerned with recordable information and knowledge, and the technologies and related services that facilitate their management and use. More specifically, information science is a field of professional practice and scientific inquiry addressing the effective communication of information and information objects, particularly knowledge records, among humans in the context of social, organizational, and individual need for and use of information. The domain of information science is the transmission of the universe of human knowledge in recorded form, centering on manipulation (representation, organization, and retrieval) of information, rather than knowing information.”Saracevic, T. (2009). Information science. In M. J. Bates (Ed.), Encyclopedia of library and information sciences (3rd ed.) (pp. 2570-2585). New York: Taylor and Francis."
    str2=input("do you remembered a word plz enter ")
    l=(len(str1))
    while True:
        num=(str1.find(str2,num,l))
        i=num
        while(i<l):
            print(str1[i],end="")
            i+=1
        print("\n\n")
        user=(input("are you satisfied ? yes or no"))
        if user=='yes':
          break
if choice==2:
str1 ="Shivaji Bhonsale I (Marathi pronunciation: [ʃiʋaˑɟiˑ bʱoˑs(ə)leˑ]; c. 1627/February 19, 1630 – April 3, 1680[5]) was an Indian ruler and a member of the Bhonsle Maratha clan. Shivaji carved out an enclave from the declining Adilshahi sultanate of Bijapur that formed the genesis of the Maratha Empire. In 1674, he was formally crowned as the Chhatrapati (emperor) of his realm at Raigad.Over the course of his life, Shivaji engaged in both alliances and hostilities with the Mughal Empire, Sultanate of Golkonda and Sultanate of Bijapur, as well as European colonial powers. Shivaji's military forces expanded the Maratha sphere of influence, capturing and building forts, and forming a Maratha navy. Shivaji established a competent and progressive civil rule with well-structured administrative organisations. He revived ancient Hindu political traditions and court conventions and promoted the usage of Marathi language.Shivaji's legacy was to vary by observer and time, but nearly two centuries after his death, he began to take on increased importance with the emergence of the Indian independence movement, as many Indian nationalists elevated him as a proto-nationalist and hero of the Hindus"

या ऑनलाईन वेबिनार मध्ये जाणून घ्या:

▶️ नेमका कोणता उद्योग व्यवसाय करावा?🧐

▶️ व्यवसाय निवडायचा कसा? त्याची पायाभरणी, उभारणी व सुरुवात कशी करायची? ☝️ 📍

▶️ सद्याच्या नवनवीन उद्योगसंधी व आत्मनिर्भर भारत अंतर्गत विविध योजनांची माहिती 📝📚

▶️ व्यवसायासाठी लागणारा प्रकल्प अहवाल, नवनवीन तंत्रज्ञान, मार्केट याबाबद्दलची संपूर्ण माहिती. 🔍🧏

▶️ उद्योगाचे व्यवस्थापन कसे करावे? आपले ध्येय निश्चित कसे करावे? 👥

▶️ भांडवल कसं उभं करतात? बँकेतून कर्ज कसं मिळवायचं?☑️

▶️ उद्योजक म्हणून यशस्वी कसं व्हायचं? यासाठी लागणारे कौशल्य आणि आत्मविश्वास कसा विकसित करावा? 😯

▶️ Finance Management कसे करावे? 💸⏳

▶️ Marketing, Sales आणि Team Management कसे करायचे? 🎯

यासारख्या अनेक प्रश्नांना उत्तर मिळवा

यासंदर्भात मार्गदर्शन करणार आहेत  ६०,००० हुन अधिक लोकांना उद्योजक बनवणारे उद्योगवर्धिनीचे संचालक *श्री.सुनील चांडक*.

( Last date to Register : 19th July 2021... Please share with 2nd /3rd /4th year students (all stream eligible) )
About Concept: Capgemini announced Tech Challenge 2021 for all Freshers/Students/Experienced candidates. Winning candidates will get Job Opportunities along with exciting prices. Tech Challenge is back with its latest edition, a unique hackathon on emerging digital technologies to engage with tech enthusiasts like you and align your skills to industry needs. The latest edition offers an array of challenges to match your skill set across multiple levels. This year promises to be more exciting than ever before !

Who Can Participate :
This challenge is open to all tech enthusiasts. If you have a flair for tech innovations, this could be your chance.
Note: This year,keeping in mind the safety aspect, Tech Challenge 2021 is going to be a 100% virtual event

What's in it for you ?
Tech Challenge is one of the largest hackathons in India.
There are prizes worth INR 20,00,000* plus a chance to land your dream job! You will also get exclusive mentoring from the tech wizards of Capgemini and an opportunity to showcase your tech skills in front of a C-suite jury; the celebrated leaders from the start-up, academia and IT industry.
Job Opportunities :
Job opportunities with Capgemini India is not entitled purely on winning the Tech Challenge 2021, and should not be considered as a final job offer. On winning the challenge, the candidate will only be given a direct opportunity for L2 interview with the HR team of Capgemini India
Prizes :
Win Prizes worth 20 lacs
How to Apply/Participate?
All candidates can register on the following Capgemini link:

http://bit.ly/CAPGEMINI_2021
Deadline to Register: Monday, 19th July 2021
Note : Please share with your students of 2nd/3rd/4th year of all branches/streams.

8/22/22, 4:03 PM - piyush bhujbal: #include<stdio.h>
int main()
{
    int n;
    scanf("%d",&n);
    int arr[n];
    for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
    {
        scanf("%d",&arr[i]);
    }
    int count=0;
    int num=arr[0];
    for(int i=1;i<n;i++)
    {
       if(num!=arr[i])
            count++;
    }
    printf("%d",count);
}

a=[int(input()) for i in range(n)]
d={}
for i in a:
 if i not in d:
  d[i]=1
 else:
  d[i]+=1
v=list(d.values())
k=list(d.keys())
for i in range(len(v)):
 if v[i]>1:
  print(k[i])
  break
 else:
  print(-1)
  break
